[3m#    + M O R E  [0m
[3m#    ---------[0m
[3m#    M O N E Y[0m
[3m#[0m
[3m#    Column [0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m [0m[1;3m([0m[3mones[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m: D + E = Y + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m#    Column [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m [0m[1;3m([0m[3mtens[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m: N + R + carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = E + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m [0m
[3m#    Column [0m[1;3;36m2[0m[3m [0m[1;3m([0m[3mhundreds[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m: E + O + carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = N + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m#    Column [0m[1;3;36m3[0m[3m [0m[1;3m([0m[3mthousands[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m: S + M + carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = O + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m#    Column [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m [0m[1;3m([0m[3mten-thousands[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m: carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = M [0m[1;3m([0m[3msince MONEY starts with M[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# For each possible combination of letter values, enforce arithmetic[0m
[3m# Column [0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m: D + E = Y + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m
[3mfor d_val in digits:[0m
[3m    for e_val in digits:[0m
[3m        for y_val in digits:[0m
[3m            sum_de = d_val + e_val[0m
[3m            # If these specific values are chosen, then the carry must be consistent[0m
[3m            if sum_de < [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:  # No carry[0m
[3m                if sum_de == y_val:[0m
[3m                    [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'D'[0m[3m, d_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'E'[0m[3m, e_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                               -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'Y'[0m[3m, y_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m            else:  # Carry = [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m                if sum_de == y_val + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                    [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'D'[0m[3m, d_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'E'[0m[3m, e_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                               -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'Y'[0m[3m, y_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Column [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m: N + R + carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = E + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m
[3mfor n_val in digits:[0m
[3m    for r_val in digits:[0m
[3m        for e_val in digits:[0m
[3m            for c0 in [0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m, [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m:[0m
[3m                sum_nrc0 = n_val + r_val + c0[0m
[3m                carry0_lit = carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m[3m if c0 == [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m else -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m                [0m
[3m                if sum_nrc0 < [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:  # No carry out[0m
[3m                    if sum_nrc0 == e_val:[0m
[3m                        [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'N'[0m[3m, n_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'R'[0m[3m, r_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                                   -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'E'[0m[3m, e_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry0_lit, -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m                else:  # Carry = [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m                    if sum_nrc0 == e_val + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                        [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'N'[0m[3m, n_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'R'[0m[3m, r_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                                   -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'E'[0m[3m, e_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry0_lit, carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Column [0m[1;3;36m2[0m[3m: E + O + carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = N + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m
[3mfor e_val in digits:[0m
[3m    for o_val in digits:[0m
[3m        for n_val in digits:[0m
[3m            for c1 in [0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m, [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m:[0m
[3m                sum_eoc1 = e_val + o_val + c1[0m
[3m                carry1_lit = carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m if c1 == [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m else -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m                [0m
[3m                if sum_eoc1 < [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:  # No carry out[0m
[3m                    if sum_eoc1 == n_val:[0m
[3m                        [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'E'[0m[3m, e_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'O'[0m[3m, o_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                                   -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'N'[0m[3m, n_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry1_lit, -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m                else:  # Carry = [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m                    if sum_eoc1 == n_val + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                        [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'E'[0m[3m, e_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'O'[0m[3m, o_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                                   -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'N'[0m[3m, n_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry1_lit, carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Column [0m[1;3;36m3[0m[3m: S + M + carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = O + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m*carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m
[3mfor s_val in digits:[0m
[3m    for m_val in digits:[0m
[3m        for o_val in digits:[0m
[3m            for c2 in [0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m, [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m][0m[3m:[0m
[3m                sum_smc2 = s_val + m_val + c2[0m
[3m                carry2_lit = carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m[3m if c2 == [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m else -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m                [0m
[3m                if sum_smc2 < [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:  # No carry out[0m
[3m                    if sum_smc2 == o_val:[0m
[3m                        [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'S'[0m[3m, s_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'M'[0m[3m, m_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                                   -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'O'[0m[3m, o_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry2_lit, -carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m                else:  # Carry = [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m                    if sum_smc2 == o_val + [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                        [0m[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3m-letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'S'[0m[3m, s_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'M'[0m[3m, m_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, [0m
[3m                                   -letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'O'[0m[3m, o_val[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m, -carry2_lit, carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Column [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m constraint: carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[3m = M [0m[1;3m([0m[3mthe leading digit of MONEY[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m# This means: if carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[3m is true, then M must be [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m# if carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[3m is false, then M must be [0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m, but M cannot be [0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m [0m[1;3m([0m[3mleading digit constraint[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m# So carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[3m must be true and M must be [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcarry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m[3m  # carry[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3;36m3[0m[1;3m][0m[3m must be true[0m
[1;3;35mwcnf.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m[[0m[3mletter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m'M'[0m[3m, [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m)[0m[3m  # M must be [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[1;3;36m3[0m[3m | # No soft constraints needed - this is a pure constraint satisfaction problem[0m
[3m# All constraints are hard requirements[0m
[1;3;36m4[0m[3m | # Solve and export solution[0m
[3mwith [0m[1;3;35mRC2[0m[1;3m([0m[3mwcnf[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m as solver:[0m
[3m    model = [0m[1;3;35msolver.compute[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m    [0m
[3m    if model:[0m
[3m        # Extract letter assignments[0m
[3m        letter_assignments = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3m        for letter in letters:[0m
[3m            for digit in digits:[0m
[3m                if letter_digit[0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m([0m[3mletter, digit[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m in model:[0m
[3m                    letter_assignments[0m[3m = digit[0m
[3m                    break[0m
[3m        [0m
[3m        # Extract carry values for debugging[0m
[3m        carry_values = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3m        for i in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            carry_values[0m[3m = carry[0m[3m in model[0m
[3m        [0m
[3m        # Verify the solution[0m
[3m        send = letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'S'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m1000[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'E'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m100[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'N'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'D'[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        more = letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'M'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m1000[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'O'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m100[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'R'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'E'[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        money = letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'M'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m10000[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'O'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m1000[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'N'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m100[0m[3m + letter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'E'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m10[0m[3m + [0m
[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'Y'[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        [0m
[3m        is_valid = [0m[1;3m([0m[3msend + more == money[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m        [0m
[3m        # Show the visual representation[0m
[3m        visual = f"[0m[3;32m""[0m
[3m  [0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'S'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'E'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'N'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'D'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m

[3m------[0m
[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'M'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'O'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'N'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'E'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mletter_assignments[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'Y'[0m[1;3m][0m[1;3m}[0m
[3;32m""[0m[3m"[0m
[3m        [0m
[3m        [0m[1;3;35mexport_solution[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m{[0m
[3m            [0m[3;32m"satisfiable"[0m[3m: [0m[3;92mTrue[0m[3m,[0m
[3m            [0m[3;32m"cost"[0m[3m: solver.cost,[0m
[3m            [0m[3;32m"letter_assignments"[0m[3m: letter_assignments,[0m

┌───────────────────┐
│ PROBLEM STATEMENT │
└───────────────────┘
# Cryptarithmetic Puzzle

Can you solve this cryptarithmetic puzzle using Z3?

```
  SEND
+ MORE
------
 MONEY
```

Each letter represents a unique digit (0-9). Find the digit assignment that makes this sum equation valid.

The leading digit of any number cannot be 0 (so S and M cannot be 0).



┌─────────────┐
│ FINAL MODEL │
└─────────────┘
0 | from pysat.formula import WCNF
from pysat.examples.rc2 import RC2
# Note: Helper functions are already available

wcnf = WCNF()
1 | # PARAMETER VERIFICATION
# Problem: SEND + MORE = MONEY
# - 8 unique letters: S, E, N, D, M, O, R, Y  
# - Each letter maps to unique digit 0-9
# - Leading digits S and M cannot be 0

letters = ['S', 'E', 'N', 'D', 'M', 'O', 'R', 'Y']
digits = list(range(10))

# Variables: letter_digit[letter][digit] = 1 if letter has value digit
var_count = 0
letter_digit = {}

for letter in letters:
    for digit in digits:
        var_count += 1
        letter_digit[(letter, digit)] = var_count

# Create variables for carries between columns
# carry[i] = 1 if there's a carry from column i to column i+1
# Column 0 = ones, 1 = tens, 2 = hundreds, 3 = thousands
carry = {}
for i in range(4):
    var_count += 1 
    carry[i] = var_count

print(f"Total variables: {var_count}")
2 | # Hard constraints

# 1. Each letter has exactly one digit
for letter in letters:
    digit_vars = [letter_digit[(letter, digit)] for digit in digits]
    for clause in exactly_one(digit_vars):
        wcnf.append(clause)

# 2. Each digit is used by at most one letter (all different constraint)
for digit in digits:
    letter_vars = [letter_digit[(letter, digit)] for letter in letters]
    for clause in at_most_one(letter_vars):
        wcnf.append(clause)

# 3. Leading digits cannot be 0
wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('S', 0)]])  # S ≠ 0
wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('M', 0)]])  # M ≠ 0

# 4. Column-wise arithmetic constraints for SEND + MORE = MONEY
#    Analyzing the equation:
#      S E N D
#    + M O R E  
#    ---------
#    M O N E Y
#
#    Column 0 (ones): D + E = Y + 10*carry[0]
#    Column 1 (tens): N + R + carry[0] = E + 10*carry[1] 
#    Column 2 (hundreds): E + O + carry[1] = N + 10*carry[2]
#    Column 3 (thousands): S + M + carry[2] = O + 10*carry[3]
#    Column 4 (ten-thousands): carry[3] = M (since MONEY starts with M)

# Since M must be the leading digit of MONEY and cannot be 0, M must be 1
wcnf.append([letter_digit[('M', 1)]])  # M = 1

# Column 0: D + E = Y + 10*carry[0]
# For each valid combination, add constraint
for d_val in digits:
    for e_val in digits:
        for y_val in digits:
            sum_de = d_val + e_val
            if sum_de == y_val:  # No carry (sum < 10)
                # If D=d_val AND E=e_val AND Y=y_val, then carry[0]=false
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('D', d_val)], -letter_digit[('E', e_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('Y', y_val)], -carry[0]])
            elif sum_de == y_val + 10:  # Carry = 1 (sum >= 10)
                # If D=d_val AND E=e_val AND Y=y_val, then carry[0]=true
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('D', d_val)], -letter_digit[('E', e_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('Y', y_val)], carry[0]])

# Column 1: N + R + carry[0] = E + 10*carry[1]
for n_val in digits:
    for r_val in digits:
        for e_val in digits:
            # Case when carry[0] = false
            sum_nr = n_val + r_val
            if sum_nr == e_val:  # No carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('N', n_val)], -letter_digit[('R', r_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('E', e_val)], carry[0], -carry[1]])
            elif sum_nr == e_val + 10:  # Carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('N', n_val)], -letter_digit[('R', r_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('E', e_val)], carry[0], carry[1]])
            
            # Case when carry[0] = true
            sum_nr1 = n_val + r_val + 1
            if sum_nr1 == e_val:  # No carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('N', n_val)], -letter_digit[('R', r_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('E', e_val)], -carry[0], -carry[1]])
            elif sum_nr1 == e_val + 10:  # Carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('N', n_val)], -letter_digit[('R', r_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('E', e_val)], -carry[0], carry[1]])

# Column 2: E + O + carry[1] = N + 10*carry[2]
for e_val in digits:
    for o_val in digits:
        for n_val in digits:
            # Case when carry[1] = false
            sum_eo = e_val + o_val
            if sum_eo == n_val:  # No carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('E', e_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('N', n_val)], carry[1], -carry[2]])
            elif sum_eo == n_val + 10:  # Carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('E', e_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('N', n_val)], carry[1], carry[2]])
            
            # Case when carry[1] = true
            sum_eo1 = e_val + o_val + 1
            if sum_eo1 == n_val:  # No carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('E', e_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('N', n_val)], -carry[1], -carry[2]])
            elif sum_eo1 == n_val + 10:  # Carry out
                wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('E', e_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                           -letter_digit[('N', n_val)], -carry[1], carry[2]])

# Column 3: S + M + carry[2] = O + 10*carry[3]
# Since we know M = 1, we can simplify
for s_val in digits:
    for o_val in digits:
        # Case when carry[2] = false  
        sum_s1 = s_val + 1  # M = 1
        if sum_s1 == o_val:  # No carry out
            wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('S', s_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                       carry[2], -carry[3]])
        elif sum_s1 == o_val + 10:  # Carry out (carry[3] = true)
            wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('S', s_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                       carry[2], carry[3]])
        
        # Case when carry[2] = true
        sum_s11 = s_val + 1 + 1  # M = 1, carry = 1
        if sum_s11 == o_val:  # No carry out
            wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('S', s_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                       -carry[2], -carry[3]])
        elif sum_s11 == o_val + 10:  # Carry out
            wcnf.append([-letter_digit[('S', s_val)], -letter_digit[('O', o_val)], 
                       -carry[2], carry[3]])

# Column 4: carry[3] = M (the leading digit of MONEY must be M=1)
# Since M=1 and the ten-thousands digit of MONEY is M, we need carry[3] = true
wcnf.append([carry[3]])  # carry[3] must be true
3 | # No soft constraints needed - this is a pure constraint satisfaction problem
# All constraints are hard requirements
4 | # Solve and export solution
with RC2(wcnf) as solver:
    model = solver.compute()
    
    if model:
        # Extract letter assignments
        letter_assignments = {}
        for letter in letters:
            for digit in digits:
                if letter_digit[(letter, digit)] in model:
                    letter_assignments[letter] = digit
                    break
        
        # Extract carry values for debugging
        carry_values = {}
        for i in range(4):
            carry_values[f"carry_{i}"] = carry[i] in model
        
        # Verify the solution
        send = letter_assignments['S'] * 1000 + letter_assignments['E'] * 100 + letter_assignments['N'] * 10 + letter_assignments['D']
        more = letter_assignments['M'] * 1000 + letter_assignments['O'] * 100 + letter_assignments['R'] * 10 + letter_assignments['E']
        money = letter_assignments['M'] * 10000 + letter_assignments['O'] * 1000 + letter_assignments['N'] * 100 + letter_assignments['E'] * 10 + letter_assignments['Y']
        
        is_valid = (send + more == money)
        
        # Show the visual representation
        visual = f"""
  {letter_assignments['S']}{letter_assignments['E']}{letter_assignments['N']}{letter_assignments['D']}
+ {letter_assignments['M']}{letter_assignments['O']}{letter_assignments['R']}{letter_assignments['E']}
------
{letter_assignments['M']}{letter_assignments['O']}{letter_assignments['N']}{letter_assignments['E']}{letter_assignments['Y']}
"""
        
        export_solution({
            "satisfiable": True,
            "cost": solver.cost,
            "letter_assignments": letter_assignments,
            "carry_values": carry_values,
            "send": send,
            "more": more, 
            "money": money,
            "equation_valid": is_valid,
            "equation": f"{send} + {more} = {money}",
            "visual_solution": visual,
            "verification": f"SEND + MORE = MONEY → {send} + {more} = {money} (Valid: {is_valid})"
        })
    else:
        export_solution({
            "satisfiable": False,
            "message": "No solution exists for this cryptarithmetic puzzle"
        })

Explanation: Looking at this MaxSAT solution for the cryptarithmetic puzzle, I'll review it systematically.

## Structural Correctness ✅

- **WCNF Usage**: Correctly uses `WCNF()` for MaxSAT
- **Hard Constraints**: All constraints properly added with `wcnf.append(clause)` without weights
- **Solver**: RC2 solver used correctly with `RC2(wcnf)`
- **Export**: `export_solution()` called with comprehensive results

## Hard Constraint Satisfaction ❌

The solution reports `equation_valid: False` with the assignment:
- S=6, E=7, N=5, D=4, M=1, O=3, R=2, Y=0
- SEND = 6754, MORE = 1327, MONEY = 13570
- 6754 + 1327 = 8081 ≠ 13570

This violates the fundamental constraint that SEND + MORE = MONEY.

## Additional Issues

1. **Incorrect Leading Digit Logic**: The code forces M=1 early on, but this seems to create conflicts with the arithmetic constraints.

2. **Constraint Encoding Problems**: While I'm not verifying the encoding logic itself, the fact that the solver returns a solution that doesn't satisfy the basic arithmetic equation suggests there are issues in how the column-wise arithmetic constraints were implemented.

3. **Missing Digit Constraint**: The code has "at most one" constraints for digits but doesn't ensure all 8 letters get different digits (it should be exactly 8 of the 10 digits are used).

## Solution Format ✅

- Includes `satisfiable: True`
- Includes cost from solver (0)
- Provides comprehensive output including visual representation
- Variable assignments are complete
- Good verification attempt (though it reveals the error)

## Critical Problem

The most significant issue is that the solution violates the core problem constraint. In a cryptarithmetic puzzle, the fundamental requirement is that the arithmetic equation holds true. A solution where SEND + MORE ≠ MONEY is fundamentally incorrect, regardless of whether it satisfies the encoded constraints.

This suggests either:
1. The constraint encoding has errors that allowed an invalid solution
2. The arithmetic verification code has errors (but 6754 + 1327 = 8081, not 13570, so the verification is correct)
